Please follow the instructions in the request for evidence. If you do not receive your request for evidence by January 18, 2023, please go to www.uscis.gov/e-request to request a copy of the notice. If you move, go to www.uscis.gov/addresschange to give us your new mailing address.

SRC2290010959
On January 3, 2023, we denied your Form I-485, Application to Register Permanent Residence or Adjust Status, Receipt Number SRC2290010959. We sent you a denial notice that explains why we denied your case and your options. Please follow the instructions in the notice. If you do not receive your denial notice by January 18, 2023, please go to www.uscis.gov/e-request to request a copy of the notice. If you move, go to www.uscis.gov/addresschange to give us your new mailing address.
